          &lt;div class="date-outer"&gt;
        
&lt;h2 class='date-header'&gt;&lt;span&gt;Thursday, 12 June 2014&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;

          &lt;div class="date-posts"&gt;
        
&lt;div class='post-outer'&gt;
&lt;div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'&gt;
&lt;meta content='http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-q3o7Ml91hB0/U5ied-X0jxI/AAAAAAAAI94/9nOIbYqUJMY/s1600/speculaas+nanaimos.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/&gt;
&lt;meta content='329952935480830193' itemprop='blogId'/&gt;
&lt;meta content='4645140496462996034' itemprop='postId'/&gt;
&lt;a name='4645140496462996034'&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'&gt;
Speculaas Nanaimo Bars (and Canada's Taste Trail)
&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header'&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header-line-1'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-4645140496462996034' itemprop='description articleBody'&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-q3o7Ml91hB0/U5ied-X0jxI/AAAAAAAAI94/9nOIbYqUJMY/s1600/speculaas+nanaimos.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"&gt;&lt;img alt="speculoos, speculaas, nanaimo, canada, anna olson, food blogger connect" border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-q3o7Ml91hB0/U5ied-X0jxI/AAAAAAAAI94/9nOIbYqUJMY/s1600/speculaas+nanaimos.jpg" height="855" title="speculaas nanaimo bars" width="570" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
Yes, Speculaas Nanaimo bars - sound good don&#8217;t they? Or
perhaps you haven&#8217;t heard of Nanaimo bars at all. They are bars of
deliciousness which originated in Canada (the city of Nanaimo to be exact). &lt;a href="http://www.cakeyboi.com/2012/07/olympic-challenge-americas-nanaimo-bars.html" target="_blank"&gt;I have made original ones before&lt;/a&gt; which comprise a biscuit base, thick custard filling
and topped with chocolate.&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-j1kqjBbjyrU/U5ievQISfYI/AAAAAAAAI-A/GLFAzcShS0Y/s1600/spice+mix.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"&gt;&lt;img border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-j1kqjBbjyrU/U5ievQISfYI/AAAAAAAAI-A/GLFAzcShS0Y/s1600/spice+mix.JPG" height="320" width="213" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
I was recently sent some spice mix to try out by a company,
&lt;a href="http://www.speculaas.co.uk/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank"&gt;The Speculaas Spice Company&lt;/a&gt;. Speculaas biscuits, or cookies, originated in the
Netherlands in the 17&lt;sup&gt;th&lt;/sup&gt; century and they have been popular ever
since. Steven who runs the company wanted to create a spice mix like the one
that has been passed down through his family. Vandotsch speculaas as it&#8217;s
called has a mix of 9 spices including cinnamon, ginger and cloves. Perfect to
be used in any number of sweet treats, I wasn&#8217;t sure initially what to conjur
up with the mix.&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Bnx73nHce-8/U5ifIynZnDI/AAAAAAAAI-I/Cu3MtRRElmo/s1600/battersea+arts+centre.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"&gt;&lt;img alt="battersea arts centre" border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Bnx73nHce-8/U5ifIynZnDI/AAAAAAAAI-I/Cu3MtRRElmo/s1600/battersea+arts+centre.JPG" height="266" title="battersea arts centre" width="400" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
Then my inspiration came whilst I was at the &lt;a href="http://www.foodbloggerconnect.com/" target="_blank"&gt;Food Blogger Connect&lt;/a&gt; conference last weekend in London. The conference, held at the
&lt;a href="https://www.bac.org.uk/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank"&gt;Battersea Arts Centre&lt;/a&gt;, was attended by food bloggers from all over and there
were labs and knowledge hubs on various topics throughout the weekend. I will
bring you more about this soon. At the conference though, was strEat party held
for the attendees to sample foods from all over the world. &lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-DcwAjynaPGc/U5ifrmon7eI/AAAAAAAAI-Q/--LM1W8KGvs/s1600/Icewine.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"&gt;&lt;img border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-DcwAjynaPGc/U5ifrmon7eI/AAAAAAAAI-Q/--LM1W8KGvs/s1600/Icewine.JPG" height="400" width="265" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
And one such country, you guessed it, was Canada. I love
Canada, although it&#8217;s been 10 years since I last visited. &lt;a href="https://twitter.com/ExploreCanada" rel="nofollow" target="_blank"&gt;Explore Canada&lt;/a&gt; was
there offering 'Canada's Taste Trail' with delicious food and drink to sample. This included Canadian wine &#8211;
which I love, but you cannot find in the UK for love nor money. There was also
Icewine, a drink made from frozen grapes. It&#8217;s a more viscose drink than
regular wine, with a slightly lower alcohol content, but my goodness is
delicious. It&#8217;s meant to be sipped slowly and savoured. The icewine martinis
on offer at the weekend were too good to turn down.&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-j7uqL1OOg_8/U5igSyjhSLI/AAAAAAAAI-Y/7BvfA3XrOhA/s1600/salmon.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"&gt;&lt;img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-j7uqL1OOg_8/U5igSyjhSLI/AAAAAAAAI-Y/7BvfA3XrOhA/s1600/salmon.jpg" height="284" width="320" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
I discovered before attending the event that one of my
favourite TV chefs was going to be there. Anna Olson, who appears on the Food
Network in her shows &#8216;Fresh&#8217; and &#8216;Bake with Anna Olson&#8217; was there serving up
flavourful grilled Canadian salmon drizzled with an ice wine syrup. Anna very graciously
let me have my picture taken with her and it was a pleasure to meet her. If you
haven&#8217;t seen her shows on Food Network, check them out!&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-4rg7vcXoWTA/U5igYvlIpbI/AAAAAAAAI-g/bRiTXtjPptI/s1600/Anna+Olson.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"&gt;&lt;img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-4rg7vcXoWTA/U5igYvlIpbI/AAAAAAAAI-g/bRiTXtjPptI/s1600/Anna+Olson.jpg" height="640" width="608" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
The last Canadian treat that I sampled were &lt;a href="http://www.nanaimobarstheoriginal.com/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank"&gt;Nanaimo bars&lt;/a&gt;
(see it does all tie up) and they came in different flavours. The middle
custard filling was flavoured with either the original, caramel, mocha or
raspberry. The caramel was my hands down favourite and I will be looking for these
when I return to London very soon (I believe you can buy them in Selfridges).
But this gave me the idea to use the speculaas mix in the bars.&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-dQCQhRqlKKU/U5ighiNglPI/AAAAAAAAI-o/P3B1FXaSEAE/s1600/nanaimo+bars.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"&gt;&lt;img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-dQCQhRqlKKU/U5ighiNglPI/AAAAAAAAI-o/P3B1FXaSEAE/s1600/nanaimo+bars.jpg" height="348" width="640" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
Upon my return I purchased the ingredients and whipped them
up to take to my friend Claire&#8217;s for dinner. Claire and her husband loved them
as I knew they would. I also took some into work and all of my colleagues were
blown away by the flavours &#8211; the chocolaty biscuit base with coconut and nuts
and then the spicy sweet filling. Everyone could taste different spices in the
mix &#8211; cinnamon, ginger and I got a bit of an anise flavour.&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ZibUfI4_zIg/U5ihWvUSqxI/AAAAAAAAI_I/U_GTgLN4mvU/s1600/Spec+nanaimos.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"&gt;&lt;img alt="" border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ZibUfI4_zIg/U5ihWvUSqxI/AAAAAAAAI_I/U_GTgLN4mvU/s1600/Spec+nanaimos.JPG" height="426" title="speculaas nanaimo bars" width="640" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
Here&#8217;s how I made them:&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
Yield Approx: 20 bars&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
Biscuit Base:&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
113 grams unsalted butter&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
55 grams granulated sugar&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
1 medium egg&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
1 teaspoon vanilla extract&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
1 tablespoon unsweetened cocoa powder&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
320 grams digestive biscuits &#8211; crushed (21 biscuits approx.)&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
90 grams desiccated coconut&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
65 grams pecan nuts chopped&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
Filling:&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
56 grams unsalted butter, softened&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
2 tablespoons milk&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
250 grams icing sugar&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
2 tablespoons custard powder&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
1 &#189; teaspoon Vandotsch Speculaas spice mix&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
Topping:&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
140 grams dark chocolate (65% min)&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
15 grams unsalted butter&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
Method:&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
Line an 8&#8221;x8&#8221; brownie tin with foil and set aside.&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
To make the base , in a bowl, place the butter, sugar, the
egg, vanilla and cocoa. Place the bowl over a saucepan of simmering water (don&#8217;t
let the base of the bowl touch the water) and gently stir the ingredients until
the butter has melted and everything has blended. Remove from the heat and stir
in the crushed digestives, coconut and pecans. Transfer the mix to the brownie
tin and press down evenly, as firmly as you can. Place the pan in the fridge
for 15 minutes to chill.&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-VMJPteqx9No/U5igtHZEqCI/AAAAAAAAI-w/WBZfCU4Sf0g/s1600/base.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"&gt;&lt;img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-VMJPteqx9No/U5igtHZEqCI/AAAAAAAAI-w/WBZfCU4Sf0g/s1600/base.JPG" height="213" width="320" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
To make the filling, combine the softened butter, milk,
icing sugar, custard and spice mix until it is a smooth spreadable paste. Add this
to the top of the biscuit base and with an off-set spatula spread evenly. Place
this into the fridge to set up, for about 30 minutes.&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-9BJwvWFZm8k/U5ig2MfakmI/AAAAAAAAI-0/WC2g_2cL1Q0/s1600/filling.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"&gt;&lt;img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-9BJwvWFZm8k/U5ig2MfakmI/AAAAAAAAI-0/WC2g_2cL1Q0/s1600/filling.JPG" height="213" width="320" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
Lastly, melt the dark chocolate and butter together over
another bowl, which is on top of simmering water. Pour the melted chocolate
over the chilled filling and again, spread evenly.&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-G5fvmpgT5Y4/U5ihF71T2EI/AAAAAAAAI-8/_E97vWfbcDQ/s1600/chocolate+mix.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"&gt;&lt;img border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-G5fvmpgT5Y4/U5ihF71T2EI/AAAAAAAAI-8/_E97vWfbcDQ/s1600/chocolate+mix.JPG" height="213" width="320" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
Place into the fridge again and chill the bars for at least
an hour before slicing up into squares.&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
The speculaas spice mix can be purchased at &lt;a href="http://www.speculaas.co.uk/"&gt;www.speculaas.co.uk&lt;/a&gt;. If you can't get hold of it there are plenty speculaas spice recipes online to try for yourself, although they won't be quite like Steven's mix!&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-broi34sd1C8/U5ihNyXqetI/AAAAAAAAI_A/O0FyEIy5Ft0/s1600/speculaas+nanaimos+5.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"&gt;&lt;img alt="" border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-broi34sd1C8/U5ihNyXqetI/AAAAAAAAI_A/O0FyEIy5Ft0/s1600/speculaas+nanaimos+5.JPG" height="426" title="speculaas nanaimo bars" width="640" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
&lt;span style="font-size: x-small;"&gt;Disclosure Statement: I was sent to the spice mix free to
sample and was not requested to make a recipe with it. Any opinions expressed
are my own.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;o:p&gt;&lt;/o:p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;div class="MsoNormal"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;

      var cursor = null;
      if (items &amp;&amp; items.length &gt; 0) {
        cursor = parseInt(items[items.length - 1].timestamp) + 1;
      }

      var bodyFromEntry = function(entry) {
        if (entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
          for (var k in entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
            if (entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].name == 'blogger.contentRemoved') {
              return '&lt;span class="deleted-comment"&gt;' + entry.content.$t + '&lt;/span&gt;';
            }
          }
        }
        return entry.content.$t;
      }

      var parse = function(data) {
        cursor = null;
        var comments = [];
        if (data &amp;&amp; data.feed &amp;&amp; data.feed.entry) {
          for (var i = 0, entry; entry = data.feed.entry[i]; i++) {
            var comment = {};
            // comment ID, parsed out of the original id format
            var id = /blog-(\d+).post-(\d+)/.exec(entry.id.$t);
            comment.id = id ? id[2] : null;
            comment.body = bodyFromEntry(entry);
            comment.timestamp = Date.parse(entry.published.$t) + '';
            if (entry.author &amp;&amp; entry.author.constructor === Array) {
              var auth = entry.author[0];
              if (auth) {
                comment.author = {
                  name: (auth.name ? auth.name.$t : undefined),
                  profileUrl: (auth.uri ? auth.uri.$t : undefined),
                  avatarUrl: (auth.gd$image ? auth.gd$image.src : undefined)
                };
              }
            }
            if (entry.link) {
              if (entry.link[2]) {
                comment.link = comment.permalink = entry.link[2].href;
              }
              if (entry.link[3]) {
                var pid = /.*comments\/default\/(\d+)\?.*/.exec(entry.link[3].href);
                if (pid &amp;&amp; pid[1]) {
                  comment.parentId = pid[1];
                }
              }
            }
            comment.deleteclass = 'item-control blog-admin';
            if (entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
              for (var k in entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
                if (entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].name == 'blogger.itemClass') {
                  comment.deleteclass += ' ' + entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].value;
                } else if (entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].name == 'blogger.displayTime') {
                  comment.displayTime = entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].value;
                }
              }
            }
            comments.push(comment);
          }
        }
        return comments;
      };

      var paginator = function(callback) {
        if (hasMore()) {
          var url = config.feed + '?alt=json&amp;v=2&amp;orderby=published&amp;reverse=false&amp;max-results=50';
          if (cursor) {
            url += '&amp;published-min=' + new Date(cursor).toISOString();
          }
          window.bloggercomments = function(data) {
            var parsed = parse(data);
            cursor = parsed.length &lt; 50 ? null
                : parseInt(parsed[parsed.length - 1].timestamp) + 1
            callback(parsed);
            window.bloggercomments = null;
          }
          url += '&amp;callback=bloggercomments';
          var script = document.createElement('script');
          script.type = 'text/javascript';
          script.src = url;
          document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(script);
        }
      };
      var hasMore = function() {
        return !!cursor;
      };
      var getMeta = function(key, comment) {
        if ('iswriter' == key) {
          var matches = !!comment.author
              &amp;&amp; comment.author.name == config.authorName
              &amp;&amp; comment.author.profileUrl == config.authorUrl;
          return matches ? 'true' : '';
        } else if ('deletelink' == key) {
          return config.baseUri + '/delete-comment.g?blogID='
               + config.blogId + '&amp;postID=' + comment.id;
        } else if ('deleteclass' == key) {
          return comment.deleteclass;
        }
        return '';
      };

      var replybox = null;
      var replyUrlParts = null;
      var replyParent = undefined;

      var onReply = function(commentId, domId) {
        if (replybox == null) {
          // lazily cache replybox, and adjust to suit this style:
          replybox = document.getElementById('comment-editor');
          if (replybox != null) {
            replybox.height = '250px';
            replybox.style.display = 'block';
            replyUrlParts = replybox.src.split('#');
          }
        }
        if (replybox &amp;&amp; (commentId !== replyParent)) {
          document.getElementById(domId).insertBefore(replybox, null);
          replybox.src = replyUrlParts[0]
              + (commentId ? '&amp;parentID=' + commentId : '')
              + '#' + replyUrlParts[1];
          replyParent = commentId;
        }
      };

      var hash = (window.location.hash || '#').substring(1);
      var startThread, targetComment;
      if (/^comment-form_/.test(hash)) {
        startThread = hash.substring('comment-form_'.length);
      } else if (/^c[0-9]+$/.test(hash)) {
        targetComment = hash.substring(1);
      }

      // Configure commenting API:
      var configJso = {
        'maxDepth': config.maxThreadDepth
      };
      var provider = {
        'id': config.postId,
        'data': items,
        'loadNext': paginator,
        'hasMore': hasMore,
        'getMeta': getMeta,
        'onReply': onReply,
        'rendered': true,
        'initComment': targetComment,
        'initReplyThread': startThread,
        'config': configJso,
        'messages': msgs
      };

      var render = function() {
        if (window.goog &amp;&amp; window.goog.comments) {
          var holder = document.getElementById('comment-holder');
          window.goog.comments.render(holder, provider);
        }
      };

      // render now, or queue to render when library loads:
      if (window.goog &amp;&amp; window.goog.comments) {
        render();
      } else {
        window.goog = window.goog || {};
        window.goog.comments = window.goog.comments || {};
        window.goog.comments.loadQueue = window.goog.comments.loadQueue || [];
        window.goog.comments.loadQueue.push(render);
      }
    })();
// ]]&gt;
    </script>
    <div id="comment-holder">

           <script type="text/javascript">
            window.followersIframe = null;
    function followersIframeOpen(url) {
      gapi.load("gapi.iframes", function() {
        if (gapi.iframes &amp;&amp; gapi.iframes.getContext) {
          window.followersIframe = gapi.iframes.getContext().openChild({
            url: url,
            where: document.getElementById("followers-iframe-container"),
            messageHandlersFilter: gapi.iframes.CROSS_ORIGIN_IFRAMES_FILTER,
            messageHandlers: {
              '_ready': function(obj) {
                window.followersIframe.getIframeEl().height = obj.height;
              },
              'reset': function() {
                window.followersIframe.close();
                followersIframeOpen("https://www.blogger.com/followers.g?blogID\x3d329952935480830193\x26origin\x3dhttp://www.cakeyboi.com/\x26colors\x3dCgt0cmFuc3BhcmVudBILdHJhbnNwYXJlbnQaBjQ0NDQ0NCIGM2Q4NWM2KgZmZmZmZmYyBjNkODVjNjoGNDQ0NDQ0QgYzZDg1YzZKBjgxYTVjNlIGM2Q4NWM2Wgt0cmFuc3BhcmVudA%3D%3D\x26postID\x3d4645140496462996034");
              },
              'open': function(url) {
                window.followersIframe.close();
                followersIframeOpen(url);
              }
            }
          });
        }
      });
    }
    followersIframeOpen("https://www.blogger.com/followers.g?blogID\x3d329952935480830193\x26origin\x3dhttp://www.cakeyboi.com/\x26colors\x3dCgt0cmFuc3BhcmVudBILdHJhbnNwYXJlbnQaBjQ0NDQ0NCIGM2Q4NWM2KgZmZmZmZmYyBjNkODVjNjoGNDQ0NDQ0QgYzZDg1YzZKBjgxYTVjNlIGM2Q4NWM2Wgt0cmFuc3BhcmVudA%3D%3D\x26postID\x3d4645140496462996034");
           </script>
